## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |

| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# gRPC C++ Channel Creation and Load Balancing Pipeline

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in grpc/grpc under src/core/ that implement the channel creation and load balancing pipeline. Specifically identify: the files defining the grpc_channel struct and CreateChannel factory, the subchannel allocation logic, the round-robin and pick-first load balancing policy implementations, the name resolution interface (ResolverFactory, Resolver), and the connectivity state machine. For each file report its path and the key class or struct it defines.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grpc--v1.68.0.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Summary

I've identified and documented **30 key C++ source files** in `src/core/` that implement the channel creation and load balancing pipeline, including:

### **Channel Components**
- **Channel base class** (`src/core/lib/surface/channel.h`) - Abstract interface for all channels
- **ClientChannel** - Core implementation managing the entire pipeline
- **ClientChannelFilter** - Legacy filter-based implementation for backward compatibility

### **Channel Creation**
- **CreateChannel factory** in `chttp2_connector.cc` - HTTP/2 channel creation

### **Load Balancing System**
- **LoadBalancingPolicy** - Abstract base class for all LB policies
- **LoadBalancingPolicyFactory & Registry** - Plugin system for policies
- **PickFirst policy** - Default sequential address selection
- **RoundRobin policy** - Even load distribution

### **Subchannel Management**
- **SubchannelInterface** - Public LB policy interface
- **Subchannel** - Internal connection management
- **GlobalSubchannelPool & LocalSubchannelPool** - Connection pooling and reuse

### **Name Resolution**
- **Resolver interface** - Asynchronous address resolution
- **ResolverFactory & Registry** - Scheme-based resolver plugins

### **Connectivity State Machine**
- **ConnectivityStateTracker** - State management and watchers

Components\\n\\n**Channel Base Class** (src/core/lib/surface/channel.h)\\n- Defines the abstract `Channel` class that serves as the base for all channel implementations\\n- Includes virtual methods for creating calls, managing connectivity state, and watching state changes\\n\\n**ClientChannel** (src/core/client_channel/client_channel.h, client_channel.cc)\\n- Core implementation of the Channel interface that manages the channel creation pipeline\\n- Orchestrates resolver creation, load balancing policy instantiation, and call destination management\\n- Maintains state trackers and manages the picker observable for subchannel selection\\n\\n**ClientChannelFilter** (src/core/client_channel/client_channel_filter.h, client_channel_filter.cc)\\n- Legacy filter-based implementation providing backward compatibility\\n- Handles resolver result changes, load balancing policy updates, and call interception\\n- Manages connectivity state tracking and coordinates with the resolver and load balancer\\n\\n### Channel Creation Factory\\n\\n**CreateChannel** (src/core/ext/transport/chttp2/client/chttp2_connector.cc)\\n- Factory function that creates `ClientChannel` instances with HTTP/2 transport\\n- Handles channel args processing and initializes the channel with appropriate credentials and options\\n- Called from grpc_channel_create() to create the low-level channel structure\\n\\n### Load Balancing Policy Architecture\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicy Base Class** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy.h, lb_policy.cc)\\n- Abstract base class for all load balancing policies\\n- Defines the interface for subchannel creation, picker generation, and configuration parsing\\n- Contains helper class for managing subchannels and their connectivity state\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicyFactory** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy_factory.h)\\n- Factory interface for creating load balancing policy instances\\n- Implementations registered with the LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry\\n- Responsible for parsing policy configuration from JSON\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy_registry.h, lb_policy_registry.cc)\\n- Central registry for all load balancing policy factories\\n- Allows plugins to register custom policies\\n- Looks up policies by name and creates instances on demand\\n\\n### Load Balancing Policy Implementations\\n\\n**PickFirst Policy** (src/core/load_balancing/pick_first/pick_first.h, pick_first.cc)\\n- Default load balancing policy that tries addresses sequentially\\n- Attempts to connect to addresses in order until one succeeds\\n- Returns a picker that always selects the first healthy subchannel\\n- Includes support for shuffling address lists and internal health checking\\n\\n**RoundRobin Policy** (src/core/load_balancing/round_robin/round_robin.cc)\\n- Distributes load evenly across all available subchannels\\n- Maintains an endpoint list derived from resolver results\\n- Returns a picker that cycles through available subchannels\\n- Supports weighted round robin and other variants through separate implementations\\n\\n### Subchannel Management\\n\\n**SubchannelInterface** (src/core/load_balancing/subchannel_interface.h)\\n- Public interface exposed to load balancing policies\\n- Allows policies to monitor connectivity state changes and manage subchannels\\n- Provides data watcher interface for backend metrics and health status\\n\\n**Subchannel** (src/core/client_channel/subchannel.h, subchannel.cc)\\n- Internal implementation of subchannel with actual connection management\\n- Maintains connectivity state, handles connection establishment/teardown\\n- Manages call destinations and coordinates with transport layer\\n- Stores connection state and communicates changes to registered watchers\\n\\n**SubchannelPoolInterface** (src/core/client_channel/subchannel_pool_interface.h, subchannel_pool_interface.cc)\\n- Abstract interface for subchannel pooling and reuse\\n- Manages subchannel lifecycle and sharing across channels\\n\\n**GlobalSubchannelPool** (src/core/client_channel/global_subchannel_pool.h, global_subchannel_pool.cc)\\n- Singleton pool shared across all channels in a process\\n- Maps subchannel keys to subchannel instances\\n- Enables subchannel reuse across multiple channels\\n\\n**LocalSubchannelPool** (src/core/client_channel/local_subchannel_pool.h, local_subchannel_pool.cc)\\n- Per-channel pool for isolated subchannel lifecycle\\n- Used when GRPC_ARG_USE_LOCAL_SUBCHANNEL_POOL is enabled\\n- Prevents sharing of subchannels across channels\\n\\n### Name Resolution Pipeline\\n\\n**Resolver** (src/core/resolver/resolver.h, resolver.cc)\\n- Abstract base class for address resolution\\n- Implements lifecycle management (Start, Shutdown)\\n- Delivers address results asynchronously through ResultHandler callbacks\\n- Processes resolver results including service config and load balancing policy config\\n\\n**ResolverFactory** (src/core/resolver/resolver_factory.h)\\n- Factory interface for creating Resolver instances\\n- Each scheme (dns, ipv4, fake, xds, etc.) has a corresponding factory\\n- Factories parse URI schemes and instantiate appropriate resolver implementations\\n\\n**ResolverRegistry** (src/core/resolver/resolver_registry.h, resolver_registry.cc)\\n- Central registry of all available resolver factories\\n- Maps URI schemes to their corresponding factories\\n- Provides lookup mechanism for creating resolvers based on target URI\\n- Supports registration of custom resolver implementations\\n\\n### Connectivity State Machine\\n\\n**ConnectivityStateTracker** (src/core/lib/transport/connectivity_state.h, connectivity_state.cc)\\n- Manages channel and subchannel connectivity state transitions\\n- Supports states: IDLE, CONNECTING, READY, TRANSIENT_FAILURE, SHUTDOWN\\n- Notifies registered watchers when state changes occur\\n- Tracks status information (error messages) associated with failures\\n- Used by both channels and subchannels to track connection health\\n\\n### Integration Flow\\n\\n1. **Channel Creation**: grpc_channel_create() \u2192 CreateChannel() \u2192 ClientChannel::Create()\\n2. **Resolver Setup**: ClientChannelFilter::CreateResolverLocked() uses ResolverRegistry to instantiate resolver\\n3. **Address Resolution**: Resolver delivers results \u2192 Load balancing policy configuration is extracted\\n4. **LB Policy Selection**: LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry creates appropriate policy (PickFirst, RoundRobin, etc.)\\n5. **Subchannel Allocation**: Load balancing policy creates subchannels via SubchannelPool\\n6. **Subchannel Connection**: Subchannels establish connections and report connectivity state changes\\n7. **Picker Generation**: Load balancing policy creates SubchannelPicker for call routing\\n8. **Call Routing**: Incoming calls use picker to select subchannel for request execution\\n9. **State Tracking**: ConnectivityStateTracker monitors overall channel health and notifies clients\"\n}\n",

\"LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry::CreateLoadBalancingPolicy\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## gRPC C++ Channel Creation and Load Balancing Pipeline\\n\\n### Overview\\nThe gRPC channel creation and load balancing pipeline in src/core/ consists of several interconnected components that work together to establish client-server connections and distribute load across subchannels.\\n\\n### Core Channel Components\\n\\n**Channel Base Class** (src/core/lib/surface/channel.h)\\n- Defines the abstract `Channel` class that serves as the base for all channel implementations\\n- Includes virtual methods for creating calls, managing connectivity state, and watching state changes\\n\\n**ClientChannel** (src/core/client_channel/client_channel.h, client_channel.cc)\\n- Core implementation of the Channel interface that manages the channel creation pipeline\\n- Orchestrates resolver creation, load balancing policy instantiation, and call destination management\\n- Maintains state trackers and manages the picker observable for subchannel selection\\n\\n**ClientChannelFilter** (src/core/client_channel/client_channel_filter.h, client_channel_filter.cc)\\n- Legacy filter-based implementation providing backward compatibility\\n- Handles resolver result changes, load balancing policy updates, and call interception\\n- Manages connectivity state tracking and coordinates with the resolver and load balancer\\n\\n### Channel Creation Factory\\n\\n**CreateChannel** (src/core/ext/transport/chttp2/client/chttp2_connector.cc)\\n- Factory function that creates `ClientChannel` instances with HTTP/2 transport\\n- Handles channel args processing and initializes the channel with appropriate credentials and options\\n- Called from grpc_channel_create() to create the low-level channel structure\\n\\n### Load Balancing Policy Architecture\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicy Base Class** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy.h, lb_policy.cc)\\n- Abstract base class for all load balancing policies\\n- Defines the interface for subchannel creation, picker generation, and configuration parsing\\n- Contains helper class for managing subchannels and their connectivity state\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicyFactory** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy_factory.h)\\n- Factory interface for creating load balancing policy instances\\n- Implementations registered with the LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry\\n- Responsible for parsing policy configuration from JSON\\n\\n**LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry** (src/core/load_balancing/lb_policy_registry.h, lb_policy_registry.cc)\\n- Central registry for all load balancing policy factories\\n- Allows plugins to register custom policies\\n- Looks up policies by name and creates instances on demand\\n\\n### Load Balancing Policy Implementations\\n\\n**PickFirst Policy** (src/core/load_balancing/pick_first/pick_first.h, pick_first.cc)\\n- Default load balancing policy that tries addresses sequentially\\n- Attempts to connect to addresses in order until one succeeds\\n- Returns a picker that always selects the first healthy subchannel\\n- Includes support for shuffling address lists and internal health checking\\n\\n**RoundRobin Policy** (src/core/load_balancing/round_robin/round_robin.cc)\\n- Distributes load evenly across all available subchannels\\n- Maintains an endpoint list derived from resolver results\\n- Returns a picker that cycles through available subchannels\\n- Supports weighted round robin and other variants through separate implementations\\n\\n### Subchannel Management\\n\\n**SubchannelInterface** (src/core/load_balancing/subchannel_interface.h)\\n- Public interface exposed to load balancing policies\\n- Allows policies to monitor connectivity state changes and manage subchannels\\n- Provides data watcher interface for backend metrics and health status\\n\\n**Subchannel** (src/core/client_channel/subchannel.h, subchannel.cc)\\n- Internal implementation of subchannel with actual connection management\\n- Maintains connectivity state, handles connection establishment/teardown\\n- Manages call destinations and coordinates with transport layer\\n- Stores connection state and communicates changes to registered watchers\\n\\n**SubchannelPoolInterface** (src/core/client_channel/subchannel_pool_interface.h, subchannel_pool_interface.cc)\\n- Abstract interface for subchannel pooling and reuse\\n- Manages subchannel lifecycle and sharing across channels\\n\\n**GlobalSubchannelPool** (src/core/client_channel/global_subchannel_pool.h, global_subchannel_pool.cc)\\n- Singleton pool shared across all channels in a process\\n- Maps subchannel keys to subchannel instances\\n- Enables subchannel reuse across multiple channels\\n\\n**LocalSubchannelPool** (src/core/client_channel/local_subchannel_pool.h, local_subchannel_pool.cc)\\n- Per-channel pool for isolated subchannel lifecycle\\n- Used when GRPC_ARG_USE_LOCAL_SUBCHANNEL_POOL is enabled\\n- Prevents sharing of subchannels across channels\\n\\n### Name Resolution Pipeline\\n\\n**Resolver** (src/core/resolver/resolver.h, resolver.cc)\\n- Abstract base class for address resolution\\n- Implements lifecycle management (Start, Shutdown)\\n- Delivers address results asynchronously through ResultHandler callbacks\\n- Processes resolver results including service config and load balancing policy config\\n\\n**ResolverFactory** (src/core/resolver/resolver_factory.h)\\n- Factory interface for creating Resolver instances\\n- Each scheme (dns, ipv4, fake, xds, etc.) has a corresponding factory\\n- Factories parse URI schemes and instantiate appropriate resolver implementations\\n\\n**ResolverRegistry** (src/core/resolver/resolver_registry.h, resolver_registry.cc)\\n- Central registry of all available resolver factories\\n- Maps URI schemes to their corresponding factories\\n- Provides lookup mechanism for creating resolvers based on target URI\\n- Supports registration of custom resolver implementations\\n\\n### Connectivity State Machine\\n\\n**ConnectivityStateTracker** (src/core/lib/transport/connectivity_state.h, connectivity_state.cc)\\n- Manages channel and subchannel connectivity state transitions\\n- Supports states: IDLE, CONNECTING, READY, TRANSIENT_FAILURE, SHUTDOWN\\n- Notifies registered watchers when state changes occur\\n- Tracks status information (error messages) associated with failures\\n- Used by both channels and subchannels to track connection health\\n\\n### Integration Flow\\n\\n1. **Channel Creation**: grpc_channel_create() \u2192 CreateChannel() \u2192 ClientChannel::Create()\\n2. **Resolver Setup**: ClientChannelFilter::CreateResolverLocked() uses ResolverRegistry to instantiate resolver\\n3. **Address Resolution**: Resolver delivers results \u2192 Load balancing policy configuration is extracted\\n4. **LB Policy Selection**: LoadBalancingPolicyRegistry creates appropriate policy (PickFirst, RoundRobin, etc.)\\n5. **Subchannel Allocation**: Load balancing policy creates subchannels via SubchannelPool\\n6. **Subchannel Connection**: Subchannels establish connections and report connectivity state changes\\n7. **Picker Generation**: Load balancing policy creates SubchannelPicker for call routing\\n8. **Call Routing**: Incoming calls use picker to select subchannel for request execution\\n9. **State Tracking**: ConnectivityStateTracker monitors overall channel health and notifies clients\"\n}\n",
